1b1(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ he badz+ra tan tra ra dza na ma/ bod skad du/ kye'i rdo rje zhes bya ba rgyud kyi rgyal po/ 
1b2(rgyud): kye'i rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
1b3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi snying po rdo rje'i btsun mo'i ba rnams la bzhugs so// 
1b4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi snying po// rje btsun gsang ba las shin du'ang ches
1b5(rgyud): na gsang ba 'ang/ de nas byecom ldan 'das kyis bka' bstsal pa/ e ma'o byang chub sems dpa' sems
2a1(rgyud): dpa' chen po// rdo rje snying po snying rje chen po legs so// rdo rje sems dpa' dang / sems dpa' chen po
2a2(rgyud): dang dam tshig sems dpa' chen po snying po'o/ kye rdo rje zhes bya ba nyon cig/ rdo rje snying pos gsol pa// gang phyir rdo rje
2a3(rgyud): sems dpa' lags// ji ltar sems dpa' chen po lags// gang gis dam tshig sems dpa' lags// bcom
2a4(rgyud): ldan 'das kyis bdag la gsungs// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// rdo rje mi phyi zhes byar brjod// sems
2a5(rgyud): dpa' srid pa gsum gcig pa// 'dis ni shes rab rigs pa yis// rdo rje sems dpa' zhes par brjod// ye shes
2b1(rgyud): chen po'i ro gang ba// sems dpa' chen por brjod par bya// rtag tu dam tshig la spyod phyir// dam tshig sems dpa' brjod par bya// rdo
2b2(rgyud): snying pos gsol pa// ming bsdus pas ni ji lta bur// gang gis kye'i rdo rje lags// he'i rnam par ci zhig bshad// badz+ra yis kyang de bzhin ci
2b3(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ he ni snying rje chen po nyid// badz+ra 'ang shes rab brjod par bya// thabs dang shes rab bdag nyid rgyud// de ni nga
2b4(rgyud): yis bshad kyis nyon// lta stangs dgug dang bda' chen dang // don byed rnam mang brjod pa dang // rings par byed dang bskyod par byed// sde rengs byed dang / 
2b5(rgyud): mngon spyod dang // ji ltar rigs pa'i rnal 'byor ma'i// bskyed dang gnas dang byed rgyu dang // don byed ye shes rnam byed dang // lha rnams ji ltar 'byung
2b6(rgyud): 'o/ he ru ka ni bskyed pa'i rgyu// dang bye gcig ni sgom par bya// rdo rje snying po snying rje che// dngos po nyid kyis rnam grol zhing // dngos pos 'ching
3a1(rgyud): bas mching bar 'gyur// de yong shes pas grol ba yin// dngos po med pa'ang yong shes par// dngos po grol 'gyur shes rab can// dngos po med par
3a2(rgyud): yong shes byas// de ltar he ru ka bsgom bya// lus la ye shes chen po gnas// rtog pa thams cad yang dag spangs// dngos po kun la khyab pa po// lus can gnas lus la
3a3(rgyud): ma skyes pa'o// kye'u bcom ldan 'das/ rdo rje'i lus lu rtse du lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rtsa rnams ni sum bcu rtsa gnyis te// byang chub kyi sems
3a4(rgyud): sum bcu rtsa gnyis dbab pa// bde ba chen po'i gnas su 'dzag pa'o// de rnams kyi nang nas rtsa rnam pa gsum ni rtse mo ste// rkyang ma dang / ro ma dang / kun
3a5(rgyud): dad ma'o// rgyang ma shes rab rang bzhin gyis// thabs kyi rom yang dag gnas// kun 'dar ma ni dbus gnas su// bzung dang 'dzin pa rnam par spangs// rkyang ma mi skyed
3a6(rgyud): dbab pa ste// ro ma de bzhin khrag 'bab cing // shes rab zla ba 'babs bshad pa// de ni kun 'dar ma rab grags// mi phyed ma dang / 'phra gzugs ma dang // rtse ba ma dang / 
3a7(rgyud): g.yon pa dang / thu du ma dang / rus sbal skyes ma dang / sgom pa ma dang / dbang ma dang / bskyed ma dang / 'jug ma dang / ma mo dang / mtshan mo dang / gsil 'dzin ma dang // 
3b1(rgyud): tshab mo dang / rgyang ma dang / kun 'dar ma dang // ro ma dang / gnos ma dang / ras ma dang / shin tu gzugs can ma dang / sgyu ma dang / rgyu sprin dang / snor bral ma dang / sru sum dang / grub ma dang / 'dod pa
3b2(rgyud): dang / de bzhin du yid bzangs ma dang / gsum bskor ma dang / 'dod ma dang / khyim ma dang / num mo dang / bdud bral mo'o// rdo rje snying pos gsel pa/ bcom ldan 'das rtsa sum bcu rtsa gnyis po 'di
3b3(rgyud): rnams ji lta bu lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ba/ srid gsum yongs 'gyur thams cad ni// bzung dang 'dzin pa rnam par spangs// yang na thabs ni thams cad kyi// dngos po'i mtshan
3b4(rgyud): nyid du ni dgas// sdom pa'i dbye ba'ang bshad par bya ste/ deli da ka li dang / zla ba dang nyi ma dang / shes rab dang thabs so// chos dang longs spyod rdzogs pa dang // sprul pa dang ni
3b5(rgyud): sku dang thugs so// e bom y-i ni e'i rnam pas lhom spyan/ bgyi rnam pas bdag mor brjod// ma ni lha mo gas gang mo// ya'i rnam pas sgrol mor brjod// sprul pa'i 'khor lo sa
3b6(rgyud): med ma 'dub ma drug btsun pa'i dam chos kyi 'khor lnga lo pad+ma ma brgyad na mi longs spyad rdzogs pa'i 'khor lo la 'dab ma bcu drug dang / bde ba chen po'i 'khor la 'dab ma sum bcu rtsa gnyis so// 
3b7(rgyud): 'khor lo dus kyi rim pas rnam par bzhag pa sad cig ma'i gzhi ni rnam pa sna rogs dang / rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par med pa dang / mtshan nyid dang bral ba'o// 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi ni/ 
3b8(rgyud): sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung dang / 'gog pa dang / lam dang / de kho na nyid pa ni ni/ bdag gi de kho na dang / sngags kyi de kho na dang / lha'i de kho na dang / ye shes kyi de kho na'o// dga' ba bzhi ni/ dga'
4a1(rgyud): dang / mchog tu dga' ba dang / dga' bral gyi dga' ma dang / lhan cig skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / sde pa bzhi ni/ gnas gtan pa dang / thams cad yod par smra ba dang / kun gyis
4a2(rgyud): bkur ba dang / kye 'dun phal chen no// zla ba dang / nyi me dang / a li dang / ka li dang / 'pho ba bcu drug dang / dbyu gu drug bcu rtsa bzhi dang / chu tshod sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang / thun tshod bzhi ste/ de ltar
4a3(rgyud): thams cad bzhi bzhi'o// lte bar nub mo 'bar ba yis// de bzhin gshegs pa lnga sregs cing // spyan la sogs pa'ang yang sregs te// sregs pas ri 'ong can haM 'dzag// rdo rje rigs kyi le'u sa
4a4(rgyud): dang pa'o// / sngags kyi le'u bshad par bya ste/ oM a kha ro mu khaM sarba d+harma nong ar nud pan ta tA oM mahU~M/ phaT swAhA/ 'byung po thams cad kyi gtor ma'i sngags so// 
4a5(rgyud): bruM o dzaM khaM hUM/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sa bon no// oM d+hi ba pe tsu badz+ra hUM hUM hUM phaT swA hA/ kye'i rdo rje'i snying po'i/ sngags thams cad kyi dang por ni/ oM gyi rnam pa dang / mthar ni
4a6(rgyud): swAh+la dang hU~M phaTe/ kyi rnam pa ni nang du 'jug go// oM ma ka tsa Tu ta ba ya sha sAh+la/ grong khyer de krig pa'i sngags so// a A i mI/ u U/ ri rI li li/ e e/ oM o/ a/ rnal 'byor ma rnams kyi sa bon
4a7(rgyud): oM trai li krI k+She pa hUM hU~M hU~M phaT sarba/ phyag gnyis pa'i snying po'o/ oM dza la dzi la b+h+yo hU~M hU~M hU~M phaT swAhA/ phyag bzhi pa yi'o// mr-i ki kai Ta~M Ti badz+ra hUM hU~M hUM phaT satwa/ phyag drug pa'i'o// oM mA hUM/ sku da
4a8(rgyud): gsung dang thugs byin gyis rlabs pa'i sngags so// oM ra rak+ShahUM hUM hU~M phaT sarba/ saM skyeng ba'i sngags so// oM hU~M sarba/ rengs par byed pa'o/ A~M a sad+ha/ dba'i du byed pa'o// oM kha~M sarba/ 
4b1(rgyud): bskyod par byed pa'o// oM badz+ri ro swahA/ sdang bar byed pa'o// oM buM swahA/ mngon spyod do// oM hUM swA hA/ 'gugs par byed pa'o// oM gu sa hA/ oM ku ru ku ru le la hI swahA/ ku ru ku lu'i sngags so// oM hUM
4b2(rgyud): swA hA/ a phu'i rnam pas mtha' yas kyi gzugs brnyan byas la/ bdud rtsi lnga yis ni blugs/ me tog nag pos ni mchod// klu 'dul bar byed pa'i khu phyogs su rdzing byas te/ mtha' yas der gzhag// 
4b3(rgyud): de'i 'gram du dkyil 'khor bzhengs par bya ste// rdung khrod kyi sol bas ni byug/ glang po che'i chang gis ni mgo bo byug/ kham par kha sbyar du gzhug/ ba nag mo'i 'o mos ni dgang / gzhon nu ma nag mos
4b4(rgyud): bkal ba'i bskud pas ni dkri/ rlung gi phyogs su rdzing byas te/ mtha' yas der gzhag go// de'i 'bram du dkyil 'khor rdo bzhengs par bya ste/ dur khrod kyi sol bas ni rdul tshon nag po// skyes
4b5(rgyud): pa'i rus pa'i phye mas ni rdul tshon dkar po// ldong ros kyis ni rdul tshon ser po// dur khrod kyi sa phag gis ni rdul tshen dmar po// ro sregs pa'i sol ba dang skyes pa'i rus pa/ 
4b6(rgyud): sngon po'o// rkun mo'i lo maM dang skyes pa'i rus pa'i phye ma dag gos ni rdul tshon ljang khu ste// rdul tshon 'di rnams kyis dkyil 'khor bzhengs so// dur khrod kyi srad bus thig gad bo cing / dkyil
4b7(rgyud): 'khor khru gsu byas te/ de'i dbus su mtha' yas kye rdo rje zhal brgyad pa// rnams bzhi pa/ phyag bcu drug gis brgyan pa/ spyan nyi shu rtsa bzhis che ba 'jigs par mdzad pa bri'o// de nas bslab
4b8(rgyud): dpon bdag nyida'i sa shin tu ma rungs pa'i sems kyis dben pa'i gnas su sngags bzlas te/ oM g+hu ru g+hu ru Tu g+hu go Ta ga Ta mo sha ma sha ga Ta g+ha Ta/ g+ho Ta ya g+ho Ta ya/ a narma kro ba karta ya na ga N+DI
5a1(rgyud): tas na saHsa rbA bA d+ha y-ig+h+na wAn tsug/ rna sar+b+ba d+hA mA~M tA r+dz+dza l+ra pu phu Tu phu phuphu thu phu thu d+hA pardzas pa/ gas te rgyur mi 'brabar/ de'i sngags 'di brnags rdos te/ dbab
5a2(rgyud): gal te mi nga de'i tshe ma a dz+wa la'i nog pa lnga legs so// nai byung zhes bye ba'i tshi ge'o// sbyin 'brel bi bshad de/ dur khrod kyi ras lanye bar 'dug nas/ sngags bla zheng dras te/ oM u
5a3(rgyud): Ad+ya zhan smra/ hU~M sus/ skyera'aja'o// rol gyi srin po par gzhig pa phyir// kha tika'i babyung bshud de/ Sha te/ deng dung rtsis dang / ku thar chenan ldan ci
5a4(rgyud): sa swA tI/ sgyogs ni/ oMbadz+ra kA / dz+ra hU~M hU~M Tasad+ha/ 'islong ba'i/ dngas chu d+ha/ dod du bya bzlas zhing / smye du smye ba 'dus smras te/ smras
5a5(rgyud): la ril ba skyi thugs kyis mgrin pa bskor zhing bser bcad na/ dekyi khrims cad kyi mgo med par 'gyur ro// rdo rje dro / gi tshiga'o// lce rnams 'did pas thig me bsgrubs te/ rangs
5a6(rgyud): pa'i sa bon rgyal la bsgrubs nas/ ku ba ra ts+tshin drang sres la/ nyi ma gzas zin pan/ mi spyod pa dang bdags cing / btags nas dgras bya ste/ de rkang pas mnan nas sngags bzlas te/ oM pradz+ra kuta ra
5a7(rgyud): pA tA ya b+hud+ha hU~M phaT sa d+ha/ bye ba bzlas nas thig yi byas te/ gang la phyag byas pa de 'gas so// lha 'gas pa'i cho gal// chabs gdung bar bye ba 'dod pas/ ana'i mo mdug dang skye che dang / tsai tre k+She khubs
5a8(rgyud): dgra'i ming bri zhing / 'bras phub kyi me la gdugs te/ sngags khri bzlas so// oM he badz+ra dzar dzA rag tu b+h+yo hU~M hU~M hU~M phaT sa/ cha ba'i tshiga'o// dri bzlas pas 'grub bo// chang sdug par bya ba'i 'dod pas// 
5b1(rgyud): bsgrub bya'i lte bar yaM gyi rnam pa bsgom zhing / maM gyi rnam par gyur pa las/ chang lto bar rnam par bsgoms te/ skyug par byed pa lhas na chang skyug go// rab tu myos ma dbang du bya bar 'dod pas/ mya ngan med pa'i/ 
5b2(rgyud): brgyud la mya ngan med pa'i 'og tu song ste/ gos dmar po dgos te/ myos byed kyi 'bras bu bza' zhing / ka mA tsi kr-i'i khu bas thig le byas nas/ sngags bzlas te// oM a mu ki mau hri b+ha si b+hi rba tu swahU~M/ khris 'ong ba
5b3(rgyud): 'gyur ro// zla ba dang nyi ma dbang du bya bar 'dod pas/ sa lu btags pa'i 'gyur ba la zla ba dang nyi ma byas nas rdo rje'i chu la bzhug cing sngags bzlas te/ oM badz+ra rko ma tsa la ma tsa ma tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha badz+ra ya hUM hUM hUM phaT/ 
5b4(rgyud): swAhA/ bye ba khrag bdun bzlas te/ nyi ma dang zla ba yang dag par gnas shing nyin mtshan bye brag med par 'gyur ro// nyi ma dang zla ba yongasu 'dzin pa zhes bya ba'i cho ga'o// oM na grA na grA zhes bya ba'i sngags 'dis
5b5(rgyud): dus ma yin pa'i dus su don bsgrub pa'i phyir// gzhon nu ma'i dmig dag la brgya rtsa brgyad mngon par sngags nas/ me tog la sogs pa'i mchod pa lngas yang dag par mchod cing / snyan gsan dbab po// 
5b6(rgyud): bcu bzhi pa 'am/ 9 brgyad pa'i snga gro'i dus su bum pa la sogs pa bzhag ci tra/ 'bru mar dang a kA'i khu ba sngags 'di nyid kyis lan/ brgya rtsa brgyad mngon par mngag go// de nas mngon par sngags pa
5b7(rgyud): a lu kA ta'i khu bo sngogs pa'i 'the bo la bskus nas/ 'bru mar gyis kyang blugs la gzhon nu ma bstan te/ nga'i rdzas sus khyer smras so// de la des smras pa/ che ge mo zhes bya bas smras pa/ khyer ro rdo rje dkar
5b8(rgyud): brecis mo// pai TuTu ya zhes b+hArbotah+ya glang pA bo la u pa ro// mar+m+me mu mA zhes brjod na stag 'gros par 'gyur ro// ti li ya ti li ya zhes brjod na/ gse 'bros par 'gyur ro// i li mi li pu phu
6a1(rgyud): nis brjod na bris pa lanor srong 'dun po'i phyag gis lag tu bstan na khyi 'gros par 'gyur ro// rdo rje dang / dkar mi dang / chu ma dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma dang / bdag med ma
6a2(rgyud): dang sa spyad malha mkha' skyed pa mas mo songs pa rdul shugs can gyis byed do// sngags kyi le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / de nas sku'i le'u bshad par bya'o// 
6a3(rgyud): dang po byams pa sgom par bya// gnyis pa stong rje bsgom bya zhing // gsum pa dga' ba bsgom pa dang // kun gyi mtha' nas btang snyoms so// yang ni stong pa'i byang chub ste// gnyis pa la ni sa bon bsdu/ 
6a4(rgyud): gsum pa la ni gzugs brtson rdzogs// bzhi pa la ni yig 'bru dgod/ ri bas tsam sngon du rnam bsgoms na// nyi der hUM 'byung sna tshogs yi ge ste// rdo rje de nyid kyis ra ba dang // gur bcing ba yang rnam pa/ 
6a5(rgyud): bsgom pa nyid// dang por ra ni rnam bsgom pa// chos kyi dbying kyi bdag nyid brjid// de ste rna la 'byor pa gnas nas/ he ru kanyid rnam par bsgom// de las byung ba'i nyid kyi 'khor/ der ni/ 
6a6(rgyud): 'i rnam pa nyid/ thabs dang shes rab rang bzhin na// hUMlas byung ba'i rdo rje ni// 'a dag nag pa 'jigs chen po// rdo rje lte ba'i dbus gnas par// yang ni drug de nyid bsgom// dzI gi rnam pardzur
6a7(rgyud): skyes nas// zhe snang bdag nyid rnam par bsam// rdo rje skye ba nas blo tsho// 'dam skyes sman po 'dra ba'i mdog/ yang na sde dang nyi ma'i mngag/ dad pas nges par rnam par bral// nam khor rje btsun gyis
6a8(rgyud): nas ni// rdo rje skye ba snying rjen/ rgyan rnams thams cad 'dzin pa yi/ lha po rkyod pa rnams kyis mchod// dkar po ri dgas mtshan ma 'dzin/ tshemadun bdud las rgyal ba'i snong// ro langs min gyi/ 
6b1(rgyud): lag ma// g+ha s+pha ri ni sman 'dzin cing // pu ka si ni rdo rje lag/ de bzhin ri khrod ma ro 'dzin// rdol pa mo ni cang de'u gdung // 'di rnams kyis ni gtso bo mchod// 'dod chags chen po'i rjes chags nas/ 
6b2(rgyud): gzung mos sru la 'byung ba nyid// a li zla ba ka li nyid// sa bon nang du son gyur pa// de nyid sems dpa' zhes byar brjod// mchog tu dga' ba'i rang bzhin can// namakha'i dkyil 'khor khyab pa yi// 
6b3(rgyud): rang gi lus 'tshungs rnam par spro// bsdus nas snying khar dgug pa na// rnal 'byor zhe sdang bdag nyid gyur// sngo dang nyi ma mtshungs pa'i mdog/ b+han du dmar po'i spyan dang ldan// skra sIr gyen du 'byi/ 
6b4(rgyud): ba dang // phyag rgya lngas ni rnam par brgyan// 'khor lo rna cha nor bu dang // lag lhub dang ni skye rags nyid// sangs rgyas lnga ni rnam dag pa// 'di rnams phyag rgya rab tu grags// sdang mig brgyad
6b5(rgyud): gnyis lo yi tshul// g.yon na rdo rje thod pa dang // g.yon pa na/ yung khwa trang kha// g.ya sa na rdo rje nag pa nyid// hUM gi yi ge/ 'don pa'i bdag/ rnal 'byor ma brgyad yongs bskor nas// 
6b6(rgyud): dur khrod du ni bgon po rol// ro gnas zhes bya'i rig pa 'dis// dur khrod zhes ni mngon par brjod// phyag bzhi bdud ni bzhi las rnam par dag pa ste// gong du brjod pa'i gzugs dang / sku mdog
6b7(rgyud): daM hUM las byeng 'o// / phyagag mod kye dang br-i na/ skyes pa'i thod pa lha dang lha min gyi khrag gis gang ba/ de bzhin du gams kyi phyag na rdo rje phag lhag ma dag gis shes rab la 'khyud pa/ shes rab rdo rje
6b8(rgyud): phag mo ni btson da 'das kyis gzugs nAnA da~M// phyag drag pa la zhal gsum pa// g.yon dmar ba/ g.yas zla ba dang nyi ma lta bu/ dang po sngon po// gcer bu gong du brjod pa'i sku mdog dang gzugs can
7a1(rgyud): rnams ni pha rol du phyim ma rnam pa mam pa'o// lag g.yon pa'i dang po na rtse gsum pa/ g.yas kyi dang po na rdo rje/ phyag g.yon gyi gnyis pa na dril bu// phyag g.yas kyi gnyis pa na
7a2(rgyud): gri lug/ lhag gis rdo rje lu gu rgyud ma la sems par 'jug pacom ldan 'das ci lta ba de ltar shes rab ste// g.yas pa dang g.yon pa na gr-i khug dang thod pa/ khams gsum gyi bdag nyid can
7a3(rgyud): gyi ro mnan bral rdo mA'i le'u ste gsum pa'i// lha dbang po skur ba'i le'u bshad par bya'o// rang gi snying khar sa bon bsam mo// sa bon las 'od zer nag po lpags bkru rnam pa'i
7a4(rgyud): gzugs kyis phyung nas/ ngas khams gsum du bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad spyan drangs lo/ lha mo brgyad kyis yang dag par mchod nas/ gsol ba btab par bya'o// oM aM b+hi shrIn du ma
7a5(rgyud): sarba ta thA ga ta mai ti zhes/ sangs rgyas de rnams he ru ka'i rnam po'i gzugs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i bdag nyid kyi/ bdud rtsi lngas gang ba'i bum pa lngas dbang skur bar bya'o// dbang
7a6(rgyud): skur ba na me tog gi char dbab par 'gyur ro// rnga'i sgra 'byung bar me/ gur gum phye char dbab par 'gyur ro// rnga'i sgra 'byung bar 'gyur ro// gzugs kyi rdo rje ma la sogs pa rnams kyis mchod par bya'o// 
7a7(rgyud): rdo rje'i klu'i spyan la sogs pa rnams kyis blang bar bya'o// dbang skur nas spyod pa na rang gi rigs kyi bdag por 'gyur// 'dis ni hI ru ka rdzogs pa nyid do// thun gsum byin gyis rlabs pa'i bsgom pa
7a8(rgyud): rnam par sgoms nas/ langs te lha'i gzugs su bzhag go// dbang gi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / de nas kho na nyid kyi le'u bshad par bya'o// ngo bo gzugs med mthong ba po yang med// 
7b1(rgyud): sgra med thos pa po yang med// dri med snyoms pa po yang med// ro med myong ba po yang med// reg med reg pa po yang med// sems med sems las byung ba yang med// skye med ma sring mo nyid/ rnam// 
7b2(rgyud): 'byor rig pas rtag tu mchod// gar ma chos ma rdo rje ma// rdol pa de bzhin bram ze ma// thabs dang shes rab cho ga yis// de nyid rig pas rtag tu mchod// ci ltar shes pa mi 'gyur bar// rab tu
7b3(rgyud): 'bad pas sten pa nyid// ma gsangs sbrul dang chom rkun dang // stag dang me'i sdug bsngal byed// rigs lnga'i phyag rgya zhes bya ba// thar pa'i rgyus ni brjod par bya// rdo rje 'dis ni bdab pa nyid/ 
7b4(rgyud): des na phyag rgya brjod par bya// rdo rje pad ma de bzhin las/ de bzhin gshegs dang rin chen nyid// snying rje chen po dam pa yi/ rigs ni rnam pa lnga ru brjod// rdo rje'i phyag rgya g.yung mo nyid// 
7b5(rgyud): de bzhin pad ma gar ma nyid// las ni chos mar rab tu bshad// de bzhin gshegs pa bram ze mo// rin chen rdol pa mo shre/ bya// phyag rgya lngar ni rnam par nges// 'di rnams de bzhin
7b6(rgyud): gshegs pa'i rigs/ mdor bsdus pas ni brjod par bya// dpal ldan de bzhin nyid gshegs shing // de bzhin slar yang gshegs pa nyid// 'dis ni shes rab rigs pa yis// de bzhin

8b1(rgyud): bde ba gang gis che ba 'dir// de'i bde ba bsam gtan brjod// de kho na nyid kyi le'u ste lnga pa'o// / de nas gzhan yang rab bshad bya// spyod pa pha rol phyin pa'i mchog/ gang gis dngos

20a3(rgyud): dngos po dngos med bde// rdo rje sems dpa' bde b+ha brjod// rdo rje snying pos gsol pa// rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i rnal 'byor 'di// de'i bde ba bde chen brjod// rdzogs pa sgom pa med pa ste/ 
20a4(rgyud): skyed pa yis nI ci zhig 'tshal// bcom ldan 'das kyis bkra' stsal pa// e ma byang chub sems dpa' che// dad pa'i shugs kyis rab tu rnams// lus kyi dngos po gang lags bde// de/ 
20a5(rgyud): khor smra bar mi nus so// khyad dang khyed byed tshul gyi/ A ni// bde bas 'gro ba khyab par byed// ci ltar me tog gnas dri// me tog dngos med shes mi 'gyur// de bzhin
20a6(rgyud): gzugs pa sogs dngos med pas// bod pa nyid kyang dmigs mi 'gyur// dngos dngos po nga ma yin// dngos po rtogs phyir sangs rgyas pa// gang zhig le los snun pa dang / rmongs
20a7(rgyud): pa gang gis nga mi shes// rdo rje btsun mo 'brug ni// e'i rnam pa'i cha byad gzugs// sangs rgyas rin rnam tog/ rde ba can du rtag tu bzhugs// 'chang b+h+yo chos kyang ngo// rang rig tshogs
20a8(rgyud): ldan nyan pa dang // 'jig rten bston pa grub byang // 'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa nga// lhan cig skyes dge' rang bzhin de// mchog dga' dge 'bral dang por ni// mun pa la ni mar me ltar// 
20b1(rgyud): de bzhin nus kyang yid ches kyis// btsun mo'i ba ga bden gnasu// ston pa sum bcu rtsa gnyis mtshan// gtso bo dbyera' byang brgyad bcur ldan// khu ba zhes bya rnam par gnas// de med pas na bde med 'gyur// 
20b2(rgyud): bde ba med na de med 'gyur// nus pa med phyir ltos dang bcas// lha'i rnal 'byor las bde ba// de phyir sangs rgyas dngos po min// de nyid dngos med tshul yang min// zhal phyag rnam pa gzugs can nyid// mchog
20b3(rgyud): tu bde bas gzugs med pas// de phyir 'gro kun lhan cig skyes// rang bzhin lhan cig skyes par 'dod// rnam par dag pa'i sems kyis ni// rang bzhin mya ngan 'das pa nyid// lha'i rnam pa'i gzugs kyis ni/ 
20b4(rgyud): bzhin lag kha dog gnas pa ni// skye ba tsam gis rnam par gnas// 'on kyang bag chags phal pas so// dug gi dum bu grang nyid kyis// skye bo thams cad 'chi bar 'gyur// dug gi de nyid
20b5(rgyud): shes pa des// dug gis dug ni byin par byed// ci ltar rlung gis zin pa de// bza' bar sran mar sbyin par bya// bzlog/ pa'i sman ni rtags pa las// rlung gis rlung la snun par byed// rnam
20b6(rgyud): rtog gis ni rnam rtog dang // srid pa nyid kye srid pa dag/ ci ltar rna par chu zhugs pa// chu gzhan gyis ni dbyung bar bya// de bzhi na dngos po'i rnam rtog kyang // rnam par nges par sbyang bar bya// 
20b7(rgyud): ci ltar tshad bas tshig pa yang // me yis yang ni gdung bar bya// de bzhin 'dod chags mes tshig pa// 'dod chags me yis gdung bar bya// skye bo mi 'azad pa'i las// gang dang gang ni 'ching 'gyur/ 
20b8(rgyud): brad thabs dang bcas pa de nyid kyis// srid pa'i 'ching ba las grol 'gyur// chags pas 'jig rten 'ching 'gyur ba// 'dod chags nyid kyis rnam grol 'gyur// bzlog pa'i bsgom pa 'di nyid ni/ 
21a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas mu stegs de mi shes// 'byung ba lnga'i rang bzhin las// dbang gnyis sbyor bas lnga ru 'gyur// dga' ba chen po gcig nyid las// dbye bas lnga ru 'gro bar 'gyur/ 
21a2(rgyud): bopol kA ko la sbyar bas// reg pas sra ba'i mtshan nyid de// sra ba gti mug ngo bo'i phyir// gti mug rnam par snang mdzad brjod// gang phyir byang sems gsher ba nyid// gsher ba chu'i khamasu brjod// 
21a3(rgyud): chu ni mi skyod gzugs kyi phyir// zhe sdang 'dren pa mi spyod pa// gnyis kyi spyod pa'i sbyor ba las// drod ni rtag tu skye bar 'gyur// 'dod chags dpag med rdo rje yin// 'dod chags drod las 'thung bar
21a4(rgyud): 'gyur// ka ko lor ni ga zhig sems// de ni rlung gi ring bzhin sem so// phra dogo don yod grub pa yin// de ni yod rlung las 'byung ba yi/ na// bde ba'i 'dod chags khrag du 'gyur// dga' ba/ 
21a5(rgyud): nam mkha'i mtshan nyid de// nam mkha' ser sna rdo rjer 'gyur// / ser sna nam mkha' las 'byung nyid// sems ni chen po gci gnyid la// rang bzhin lnga yis rnam par mtshon// rigs// 
21a6(rgyud): ni lnga po de nyid lnga// stong phrag rgya bo de nyid las// de phyir 'di dag rang bzhin gcig/ bde chen mchog du phan pa nyid// 'dod chags la sogs spos lnga yis// dbye bas lnga ru 'gro bar 'gyur// gang
21a7(rgyud): gaklung ba cu je snyed kyi// rigs gcig la ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs// rigs kyi tshogs la rigs ni du ma rnams// de rnas rigs la rigs ni rnam pa brgya// de rnaMs la'ang 'bum phrag rigs chen
21a8(rgyud): rnas// bye ba'i rigs la grangs ni med par 'gyur// de yis rigs la grangs med rigs rnaMs nyid// mchog tu dga' ba'i rigs las 'byung ba rnams// kyai rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma dra ba sdom pa las// dngos
21b1(rgyud): grub brtan la phan bab pa'i// ka/ le'u zhes bya ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas rdo rje can gyi rnal 'byor ma rnaMs// rgyud thams cad kyi gleng bzhi zhes bya ba'i thabs bka' stsal pa// sdom pa dang / 
21b2(rgyud): ni dbang dang yang // de bzhin gsang ba'i skad nyid dang // dga' dang skad cig dbye ba dang // gzhan yang bza' ba la sogs pa// de la sdom pa bka' stsal pa// sangs rgyas kun gi sdom pa yin/ e
21b3(rgyud): de rnam par rab tu gnas/ e baM rno ba'i bde chen po// dbang las yang dag shes par 'gyur// de nas rnal 'byor ma rnaMs kyis/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' la 'di skad gsol to// 
21b4(rgyud): bcom ldan ston pa 'gro ba'i bla// mkha' 'gro ma yi sdom pa nyid/ e baM rnam pa ci zhes brjod// rim pa ji ltar ga sh+thad du gsol// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ e'i cha byad bzang po/ 
21b5(rgyud): gang // dbu su bau gis rnam par rgyan// bde ba thas cad kyi ni gnas// sangs rgyas rin chen za ma tog/ skad cig dbye ba sa che ba nyid// dga' ba de nyid las skye bar 'gyur// skad
21b6(rgyud): cig shes nas bde shes pa// e baM rnaM bar rab tu gnas// sna tshogs dang ni rnam smin dang // rnam nyid de bzhin mtshan nyid bral// skad cig bzhi ni rab shes pa// de ltar rnal 'byor pas
21b7(rgyud): shes par 'gyur// mkhyud dang 'o byed la sogs pa// sna tshogs rnam pa sna tshogs ga shad// rnam par smin pa de las zlog/ bde ba'i ye shes za ba nyid// bdag gi bde ba zos pa'o// 
21b8(rgyud): gros ni rnam par nyed par brjod// mtshan nyid bral ba gsuM las gzhan// chags dang chags dpral rnam par spangs// sna tshogs dang po'i dga' ba nyid// rnam smin la ni mchog dga' nyid
22a1(rgyud): rnam rnyed dga' bral dga' ba nyid// mtshan bral lhan cig skyes dga' nyid// slob dpon gsang ba shes rab dang // byazhi po de yang de bzhin no// dbang ni bzhi'i grangs kyis ni// dga' ba
22a2(rgyud): la sogs rim shes bya// rjod pa dag pa slob dpon nyid// lte ba gsang ba de bzhin no// lag bcad nas ni shes rab nyid// gnyis gnyis mkhrud la de'ang nyid// seMs can rnaMs kyi dngos grub phyir// 
22a3(rgyud): dbang ni rnam pa bzhi ru gshad// gtor dang klags pa zhes bya nyid// des na dbang zhes brjod par bya// shes rab bcu drug lon pa la// lag pa dag gis yang dag 'khyud// rdo rje dril bu mnyam sbyor bas
22a4(rgyud): slob dpon dbang du rab tu brjod// shin tu bzhin bzangs migayangs ma// gzugs dang lang mtshos rnam par brgyan// the bon lag dag gis ni// slob ma'i kha ru ltung bar bya// mam
22a5(rgyud): pa'i ro de shes pa'i phyir// ston pas shes rab rab tu mchod// mchod par byas nas gtad par bya// ston pas smras pa sos dpa' che// phyag rgya bde ba ldan pa khyer// khwa dog khro ba
22a6(rgyud): rnam spangs pa'i// slob ma cher gyur shes nas ni// ston pas de la snang ba sbyin// dbang po gnyis sbyor rdo rje 'dzin// ji ltar dbang skur gsol gdab pa'i// slob ma'i bya ba gshad par bya/ 
22a7(rgyud): bla ma phyag rgya ldan mthong nas// stod dang mchod pa ci bzhin bya// bcom ldan zhi ba chen po kye// rdo rje rnal 'byor gcig gzhed pa// mi phyed phyag rgya sgrub pa po// rdo rje rnal 'byor las 'byung / 
22a8(rgyud): ba/ ci ltar khyod ni bdag nyid che// mnga' bdag bdag la'ang de ltar mdzad// 'khor ba dam gi tshogs dag du// bying ba bdag med bdag la skyobs// zhim pa'i za ba'i dung ba dang // tshe
22b1(rgyud): dang sha chen mchog dag dang // bdug pa lhag shos 'phreng ba dang / dril bu rgyal mtshan byug pa yis// 'di rnams mchod pa rnams kyis ni// slob mas rdo rje 'dzin pa bachod// mchog tu
22b2(rgyud): dga' ba yang dag thog/ sna tshogs spangs pa'i skad cig la// ston pas smras pa sems dpa' che// bde ba chen po rnam par bzung // ji srid byang chubar du ni// sos can don gi rdo rje 'dzin
22b3(rgyud): slob ma snying rje can mthong nas// rdo rje can gyis 'di skad smras// 'di nyid ye shes chen po nyid// thams cad 'dus la rnam par gnas// gnyis dang gnyisu med pa'i tshul// dngos dang dngos
22b4(rgyud): med bdag nyid gtso// gtan dang g.yo ba khyab nas gnas// sgyu ma'i gzugs can nyid du 'dod// dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i thabs kyis ni// rtag tu nges par 'gro bar 'gyur// de nas rdo rje snying pos
22b5(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma dzes la bzod par gsol nas// bcom ldan 'di/ shel 'di skad ces gsol to// dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i ci zhes brjod// sangs rgyas kun bdag grong khyer la// bcom ldan
22b6(rgyud): bdag ni 'khrul 'gyur las// rim pa ji ltar gshad du gsol// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// dkyil 'khor snying po zhes brjod do// byang chub seMs ni bde chen po// len cing / 
22b7(rgyud): 'dzin pa byed pa'i phyir// 'dus pa dkyil khor nyid du brjod// 'khor lo zhes gnas nam mkha'i khas// yul la sogs pa rnam par sbyong // po la ka ko la sbyor bas// de'i bde ba shes par 'gyur// 
22b8(rgyud): rdo rje snying byos gsol pa// sdom bya zhes bya gang gis dang // dam tshig gis ni gnas par bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal po// khyod kyis srog chags gsad pa dang // dzun gi tshig kyang smra ba/ 
23a1(rgyud): dang rta khyod kyis ma sbyin par yang blangs pha rol bud med sten par gyis// sems gcig srog chags gsod pa nyid// gang phyir srog ni semasu brjod// 'jig rten sprul pa zhes
23a2(rgyud): rdzun gi tshig du rab tu grag ste// btsun mo'i khub ma byin par // gzhan gi bud med rang 'tshung 'dzes// de nas rnal 'byor ma thams cad kyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// 
23a3(rgyud): yum ra~M nas yang ci logs / khri dbang po rnams ni gang lags/ skye mched nas ni gang lags/ phung po nas ni gang lags/ khams rnaMs de yang ci lags/ 'di rnams kyi rang bzhin ni ci lag/ 
23a4(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// yul drug ni gzugs dang sgra dang dI dang ni// ro dang de bzhin reg bya nyid// chos kyi khas kyi rang bzhin nyid// 'di rnas yul rnaMs drug du brjod// dbang po
23a5(rgyud): rnas ni 'di drug ste// mig dang na bis+t+ra dang ni// lci dang lus da de bzhin yid// 'di ni dbang po drug po ni// gti mug lha sogs lnga na// yul dang yul can dag gis ni// skye mched bcu gnyis
23a6(rgyud): dag tu 'gyur// phung po lnga ni gzugs la sogs mthar ni rnaMgs rdo rje che// dbang yi ni yul nyid dang // dbang po rnam pA shes pa nyid// rnal 'byor ma rnaMs go tsa'i byar// khams ni bco brgyad dag tu
23a7(rgyud): rang bzhin gdod nas ma skyes pa/ rdzun min bden min de bzhin du// thams cad chu'i zla ba bzhin// rnal 'byor mas ni 'dod shes gyis// 'di lta ste banub shing dang / btsub bstan dang / skyes bu
23a8(rgyud): lag pa'i rtsol ba las/ blo bur du ma skye bar 'gyur/ me ni btsub shing dang / btsupa bstan dang / skyes bu'i lag pa'i rtsol ba las/ blo bur du me skye bar 'gyur/ me de ni gtsub la yang mi gnas/ 
23b1(rgyud): gtsub bstan la yang mi gnas/ skyes bu'i lag pa dag la yang ma yin te/ rnam pa thas du yongasu btsal na/ gcig la yang yod pa ma yin pas/ me de la yang bde ba yang ma yin/ brdzun pa yang ma

23b3(rgyud): pa/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' la mchod pa byed/ dbang po gnyis sbyor bas rjesu chags par byed/ bdud rtsi lnga'i ro yang mthung bar byed do// de nas bcom ldan 'das dges nas/ 
23b4(rgyud): rang byin gyis rlab pa snyan pa/ kye kye rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma// sangs rgyas kun gyis phyag mdzad ma'i// de nyid bodag gis gsangs mdzad pa'i// rdo rje mchod pa'i byin brlabs kyis// gshad pas 'dod
23b5(rgyud): pas rab tu nyon// lha mo thams cad dga' bar 'gyur// rangs ga par gyur te pus mo g.yas pa'i lhang nge sa lnga btsugs nas/ bcoM ldan 'das ga la ba der thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ 
23b6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung nyan to// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ bza' btung ji ltar rnyed pa dang // 'gro dang mi 'gro mi spong zhing // khrus dang gtsang sgra mi bya ste// grong
23b7(rgyud): gi chos ni rang tu yang // blo ldan sngags nyid mi zla zhing // bsam gtan nyid ni dmigs mi bya// gnyid ni spang bar mi bya ste// dbang po rnaMs ni mi dgag go// b+ha la thas cad gza' bar bya// kha
23b8(rgyud): dog lnga la mnyam par spyad// dogs pa med pa'i sems kyis ni// btsun mo thams cad dga' bar byed// mdza' bo sdug par mi bya zhing // de bzhin sdug la zhe sdang nyid// rdo shing 'jim pa'i
24a1(rgyud): bdag nyid kyi/ lha rnas la ni phyag mi bya// g.yung mo 'dol bkro lpags mkhan// phyag dang mkhan sogs rag ring dang // bram ze rje'u rmangs rigs rnas// bdag gi lus ltar reg pa nyid
24a2(rgyud): bdud rtsi lnga dang bu ram chang // dug dang nim pa bu ces skyes// skyur dang dang ra dang ska la sogs// kha ba lan tsa tsha ba dang // dri nga dri zhim mchi brnag dang // byang chub sems kyis rab tu bza'// gnyis med ye
24a3(rgyud): shes sos kyis kyis ni// mi ba cung zad yod ma yin// rang byung mi tog rnyed nas ni// pad ma'i snod du gzhag pa dang // lud pa dang ni snabs dag gis// spos nas gartul zhugs can gyis btung // smad g.yos
24a4(rgyud): kha dog sna tshogs dang // ro sreg thal bas de bzhin brgyan// me tog yi dgas gnas rnyed pas// mgo skyes legs par bcing bar bya// de nas rdo rje snying pos gsol pa// thos cad kyi rnam dag pa// bcom ldan
24a5(rgyud): 'das kyis sngar gsungs na// nges par dbang po drug gi grangs// rnam par dag pa ma mdzad pa// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// mig la gti mug rdo rje me// rna bar zhe sdang rdo rje ma/

24b1(rgyud): gshad kyis// khyod ni rtse gcig yid kyis nyon// mthan chang b+ha la shA// 'du ba ma la dza zhes brjod// 'gro ba khe ta ro ni sha// rus pa'i brgyan ni ni ra shu// 'od ba phre kha nang du brjod// cad de'u khri

24b3(rgyud): nam// sho pa tsa ru sa ma brjod// tsaM ba ka du re zhes brjod// rang 'byu si he shes khar byan khu be ka pu ru zhe su brjod// sha chen sha li dzam zhes brjod// dbang po gnyis sbyor kun tu ru zhes//

24b5(rgyud): marda rje'i rigs pa shad k+Sha gar mA de bzhin pad+ma ma'i rigs/ mchod mam no rnon chen rigs// gnyis bskyes de bzhin gshes par rjod// rjes ma lus kyi rlogs nyid de//

24b7(rgyud): khyod la gang gshad pa khongade rnams thos cad gus pas bzung // kye rdo rje 'di ni dbang skur gang // gsang ba'i skad kyis mi smra bar// 'di'i dam tshig nyis par ni// 'gyur bar 'di la the tsom med
24b8(rgyud): mi da ldan pa dag / dzin dang dang mis kyis rgyag ga nyi sangang rgya gabang rmeg mi gdu nas thongs par dzug 'ang ga ni cig rigs rnyed pa/ ma tshig ma rnam
25a1(rgyud): skyes rnal 'byor ma// da'i rkyen 'gro bar byed// kye rdo rje mkha' 'gros 'dra ba'i sgom ba las// rgyud thams cad kyi gling ba ni dang // gas pa'i skad ces bya ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o//

25a3(rgyud): spyod pa'i le'u las gang gshad pa// klu dang gar ni dngos grub sbyin// de la bdag ni the tsom mchis// klu ni ci lags gar ni ci// lha dbang skur ba'i le'u gang gsungs pa// bdag med la sogs sa bon nyid// de la
25a4(rgyud): bdag ni 'khrul pa 'khrungs// gang gis sa bon sa bon gang // rigs kyi le'u las gang bshad pa// bcu drug gnyis kyi bdag nyid rtso// bcoM ldan bdag ni 'khrul gyur pas// de rnaMs rno dag gshad du gsol// bcoM ldan 'das kyis
25a5(rgyud): bka' stsal pa/ ko la mi ri T+Ti a pro la/ mU mu ni re ka k+ko lA g+ha na ko to badz+ra i/ ku ru ni gau a i na ro la nitahi pa la khA dz+ha hi/ ge TaM ma A nAdz+dza a i/ ta le ka li ny+dza ra sa ni a i/ d+hu d+hu radz+dza
25a6(rgyud): a i tsa u sa mra ka tsu ri si hA/ si hU~M ka bu s+phu ri lA si a i mA la/ oM oMn d+ha Na sA lidz+dza/ ta hi b+hu ru kha bi a i/ b+h+r-i khA Na khe/ kar n+te/ a shud+d+ha i shud+d+hA na man+t+ri a i/ ni rang su arge tsi li/ 
25a7(rgyud): ta ti dza sa ra pa wi sa nI a i/ ma la a dzaM kun d+hu ru bar+N+Na a i/ TI nI ma d+hA hin badz+ra a a~M// dran pa dang ni mi 'phrogs rnal 'byor pas// he ru ka'i gzugs kyis kang // chags bram/ 
25a8(rgyud): min rnams sems kyis ni// 'dod chags sems kyis bzhom pa cid// ni rnams dbya sangs rgyas dang / nal 'byor ma dang ma mo mos// klu dang ga ni 'di dag gis galegs par grub nga
25b1(rgyud): da / 'ad nyid kyis no phyogs srung dang // de bzhin kyang bzung ba zhing// 'dis ste 'jig rten dbyung du / desan sngags kyi rnas pa 'ing // nga du bus dang nalen dang / gang dru
25b2(rgyud): gar byed dong // tshogs kyi bdag por grang byas nas// de la dri ni mtshon par bya// sgrog pa'i dri ni dang po nyid// de nas yang ni bya rmed dri// gzur ma la ya tsa nyid// ngang ba dang ni bung ba'i sgra// klu'i mtha' nas nyan par
25b3(rgyud): bya kha lang tso'i sgra yang ni// phyi rol tu ni mtshon bya ba// klu'i byin rlabs/ mtshon nyid do// phyag rgya rtags dang mtshan ma ste// 'dis ni rigs ni mtshon par bya// rigs 'chos sgo ba'i sbyor ba las// dngos grub med cing sgrub

42b1(rgyud): bar mdzad pa'o// thugs kyi rdo rje las byung ba'i// sems can sna tshogs rang bzhin can// sems ni rang gi rnam rtog gi// dri mas skye bo sbags par byas// de phyir kun tu rab 'bad pas// zugs kyi rdo rje rnam par
